2158 arm_status arm_rfft_init_q15(
2159  arm_rfft_instance_q15 * S,
2160  arm_cfft_radix4_instance_q15 * S_CFFT,
2161  uint32_t fftLenReal,
2162  uint32_t ifftFlagR,
2163  uint32_t bitReverseFlag)
2164 {
2165 
2166  /* Initialise the default arm status */
2167  arm_status status = ARM_MATH_SUCCESS;
2168 
2169  /* Initialize the Real FFT length */
2170  S->fftLenReal = (uint16_t) fftLenReal;
2171 
2172  /* Initialize the Complex FFT length */
2173  S->fftLenBy2 = (uint16_t) fftLenReal / 2u;
2174 
2175  /* Initialize the Twiddle coefficientA pointer */
2176  S->pTwiddleAReal = (q15_t *) realCoefAQ15;
2177 
2178  /* Initialize the Twiddle coefficientB pointer */
2179  S->pTwiddleBReal = (q15_t *) realCoefBQ15;
2180 
2181  /* Initialize the Flag for selection of RFFT or RIFFT */
2182  S->ifftFlagR = (uint8_t) ifftFlagR;
2183 
2184  /* Initialize the Flag for calculation Bit reversal or not */
2185  S->bitReverseFlagR = (uint8_t) bitReverseFlag;
2186 
2187  /* Initialization of coef modifier depending on the FFT length */
2188  switch (S->fftLenReal)
2189  {
2190  case 8192:
2191  S->twidCoefRModifier = 1u;
2192  break;
2193  case 2048u:
2194  S->twidCoefRModifier = 4u;
2195  break;
2196  case 512u:
2197  S->twidCoefRModifier = 16u;
2198  break;
2199  case 128u:
2200  S->twidCoefRModifier = 64u;
2201  break;
2202  default:
2203  /* Reporting argument error if rfftSize is not valid value */
2204  status = ARM_MATH_ARGUMENT_ERROR;
2205  break;
2206  }
2207 
2208  /* Init Complex FFT Instance */
2209  S->pCfft = S_CFFT;
2210 
2211  if(S->ifftFlagR)
2212  {
2213  /* Initializes the CIFFT Module for fftLenreal/2 length */
2214  arm_cfft_radix4_init_q15(S->pCfft, S->fftLenBy2, 1u, 1u);
2215  }
2216  else
2217  {
2218  /* Initializes the CFFT Module for fftLenreal/2 length */
2219  arm_cfft_radix4_init_q15(S->pCfft, S->fftLenBy2, 0u, 1u);
2220  }
2221 
2222  /* return the status of RFFT Init function */
2223  return (status);
2224 
2225 }
